### BQ Local Cache (DuckDB) ‚Äî gi·∫£m BQ latency cho fleet (2026-06-25)
- **C∆° ch·∫ø**: 12 b·∫£ng BQ ‚Üí parquet local (`data/bq_cache/`), query qua DuckDB thay v√¨ network. T·ªëc ƒë·ªô: 10-130ms/query (vs 5-15s BQ).
- **K√≠ch ho·∫°t**: env var `BQ_LOCAL_CACHE=data/bq_cache` ‚Üí m·ªçi l·ªùi g·ªçi `bq()` (t·ª´ `simulate_holistic_nav.py`) t·ª± route sang DuckDB.
- **ƒê√£ wire**: `wc_env.sh` (t·∫•t c·∫£ cron jobs) + `dispatch.sh` (t·∫•t c·∫£ fleet agent dispatch). M·ªçi script d√πng `bq()` ƒë·ªÅu ƒëi qua cache t·ª± ƒë·ªông.
- **Sync daily**: cron 23:45 ICT (`sync_bq_cache_daily.sh --delta`). Verify so s√°nh row count + max date vs BQ; manifest ph·∫£i `verified=true` tr∆∞·ªõc khi cache ƒë∆∞·ª£c d√πng.
- **B·∫£ng l·ªõn**: `ticker` (3.47M rows) l∆∞u per-year (`data/bq_cache/ticker/YYYY.parquet`), DuckDB ƒë·ªçc glob. `ticker_prune` (752K) l√Ý single file.
- **SQL translation**: SAFE_DIVIDE‚Üímacro, INT64‚ÜíBIGINT, DATE_DIFF‚ÜíDATEDIFF, ARRAY_AGG‚ÜíARG_MAX, DATE_TRUNC/DATE_SUB/DATE_ADD, FORMAT_DATE‚Üístrftime. VARCHAR‚ÜíDATE auto-cast cho c·ªôt date.
- **Fallback**: n·∫øu cache ch∆∞a verify ho·∫∑c thi·∫øu b·∫£ng ‚Üí `bq()` v·∫´n g·ªçi BQ b√¨nh th∆∞·ªùng (kh√¥ng b·ªã g√£y).
- **Files**: `bq_local_cache.py` (engine), `sync_bq_cache.py` (sync+verify), `sync_bq_cache_daily.sh` (cron wrapper).
